###  AddAuthorToResourceAsync\(Guid, Guid\)

Adds a person as an author to a resource.

\<example>
For example:
\<pre>\<code class="lang-csharp">await AddAuthorToResourceAsync(exampleResourceId, examplePersonId);\</code>\</pre>
\</example>

###  GetTagPageAsync\(int, int, Expression\<Func\<Tag, object\>\>?, bool, Expression\<Func\<Tag, bool\>\>?\)

